| File | Role |
|---|---|
| `pkg/kubeapiserver/authenticator/config.go` | **Primary chain builder.** `Config.New()` assembles all enabled authenticators into the ordered union pipeline. | `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/authentication.go` | CLI/config-file option structs (`BuiltInAuthenticationOptions` and per-method sub-structs). `ToAuthenticationConfig()` converts flags → `Config`; `ApplyTo()` wires the chain into the generic server. |
| `staging/.../authenticatorfactory/delegating.go` | `DelegatingAuthenticatorConfig.New()` — same structural pattern for extension/aggregated API servers. |
| `staging/.../authenticatorfactory/loopback.go` | `NewFromTokens()` — loopback authenticator for in-process clients. |
| `staging/.../authenticatorfactory/requestheader.go` | `RequestHeaderConfig` struct shared by both chain builders. |
| `staging/.../endpoints/filters/authentication.go` | `WithAuthentication()` HTTP middleware — the entry point that calls the chain on every request. |
